--Removing Impossible Evolutions--
POLIWHIRL       -> POLITOED        at level 37
KADABRA         -> ALAKAZAM        at level 37
MACHOKE         -> MACHAMP         at level 37
GRAVELER        -> GOLEM           at level 37
SLOWPOKE        -> SLOWKING        using a WATER STONE
HAUNTER         -> GENGAR          at level 37
ONIX            -> STEELIX         at level 30
SEADRA          -> KINGDRA         at level 40
SCYTHER         -> SCIZOR          at level 30
PORYGON         -> PORYGON2        at level 30
CLAMPERL        -> HUNTAIL         at level 30
CLAMPERL        -> GOREBYSS        using a WATER STONE

--Making Evolutions Easier--
Friendship evolutions now take 160 happiness (was 220).
RHYHORN         now evolves into RHYDON               at minimum level 40
HORSEA          now evolves into SEADRA               at minimum level 30
DRAGONAIR       now evolves into DRAGONITE            at minimum level 40
PUPITAR         now evolves into TYRANITAR            at minimum level 40
ARON            now evolves into LAIRON               at minimum level 30
LAIRON          now evolves into AGGRON               at minimum level 40
TRAPINCH        now evolves into VIBRAVA              at minimum level 30
VIBRAVA         now evolves into FLYGON               at minimum level 40
SNORUNT         now evolves into GLALIE               at minimum level 40
SPHEAL          now evolves into SEALEO               at minimum level 30
SEALEO          now evolves into WALREIN              at minimum level 40
SHELGON         now evolves into SALAMENCE            at minimum level 40
METANG          now evolves into METAGROSS            at minimum level 40

--Removing Timed-Based Evolutions--
EEVEE           -> ESPEON          using a SUN STONE
EEVEE           -> UMBREON         using a MOON STONE

--Random Starters--
Set starter 1 to MAREEP
Set starter 2 to PINSIR
Set starter 3 to CRADILY
